components that handle manifest signing, signature validation, and unsigned plugin allowlist enforcement.\\n\\n**Manifest Signing and Reading (pkg/plugins/manager/signature/manifest.go):**\\nThe `Signature` type implements the `SignatureCalculator` interface. The `Calculate` method orchestrates the signature verification process by reading the MANIFEST.txt file from each plugin's filesystem using `ReadPluginManifestFromFS`. The manifest is parsed via `readPluginManifest` which uses OpenPGP's clearsign.Decode to extract both the plaintext manifest JSON and the cryptographic signature. The `validateManifest` function verifies the manifest structure contains required fields and calls `Verify` to validate the PGP signature using public keys retrieved via the `KeyRetriever` interface. The `verifyHash` function validates individual plugin file hashes against the manifest's file records using SHA256.\\n\\n**Signature Validation (pkg/plugins/manager/signature/signature.go):**\\nThe `Validation` type implements the `Validator` interface. The `ValidateSignature` method checks if a plugin's signature is valid by examining the `SignatureStatus` field. For unsigned plugins, it consults the `PluginLoaderAuthorizer` via `CanLoadPlugin`. The validator handles signature inheritance for child plugins and returns appropriate errors for invalid, modified, or unsigned plugins.\\n\\n**Unsigned Plugin Allowlist Enforcement (pkg/plugins/manager/signature/authorizer.go):**\\nThe `UnsignedPluginAuthorizer` implements the `PluginLoaderAuthorizer` interface. The `CanLoadPlugin` method checks if an unsigned plugin is permitted by: (1) checking if DevMode is enabled (allows all), or (2) checking if the plugin ID matches any entry in `cfg.PluginsAllowUnsigned`. This allowlist is configured in pkg/setting/setting_plugins.go where it reads the `allow_loading_unsigned_plugins` setting from the INI configuration file.\\n\\n**Key Retrieval (pkg/services/pluginsintegration/keyretriever/):**\\nThe key retrieval system is dual-layered. The static key retriever (pkg/plugins/manager/signature/statickey/static_retriever.go) provides a hardcoded public key with ID '7e4d0c6a708866e7' used for verifying Grafana-signed plugins. The dynamic key retriever (pkg/services/pluginsintegration/keyretriever/dynamic/dynamic_retriever.go) fetches and caches public keys from the grafana.com API (`/plugins/ci/keys` endpoint), storing them in a KeyStore (pkg/services/pluginsintegration/keystore/keystore.go) that uses the infra kvstore. The service wrapper (pkg/services/pluginsintegration/keyretriever/retriever.go) delegates to either dynamic or static retrieval based on configuration.\\n\\n**Plugin Loading Pipeline Integration:**\\nThe bootstrap stage (pkg/plugins/manager/pipeline/bootstrap/steps.go) calls the `SignatureCalculator.Calculate` method during plugin construction to determine each plugin's signature status before it's added to the registry. The validation stage (pkg/plugins/manager/pipeline/validation/steps.go and pkg/services/pluginsintegration/pipeline/steps.go) applies the `SignatureValidationStep` which invokes the `Validator.ValidateSignature` method, rejecting plugins that fail signature verification unless they're in the unsigned allowlist and DevMode is enabled.\\n\\n**Data Models (pkg/plugins/models.go):**\\nPlugins track four signature statuses: `SignatureStatusInternal` (core plugins), `SignatureStatusValid` (valid signature), `SignatureStatusInvalid` (bad signature), `SignatureStatusModified` (valid signature but content mismatch), and `SignatureStatusUnsigned` (no MANIFEST.txt). Signature types include `SignatureTypeGrafana`, `SignatureTypeCommercial`, `SignatureTypeCommunity`, `SignatureTypePrivate`, and `SignatureTypePrivateGlob` for URL pattern matching.\\n\\n**Configuration (pkg/plugins/config/config.go, pkg/setting/setting_plugins.go):**\\nThe `PluginManagementCfg` holds `PluginsAllowUnsigned` (list of plugin IDs allowed to load without signatures), `DevMode` (allows all plugins), and public key retrieval settings. Configuration is read from the `[plugins]` section with key `allow_loading_unsigned_plugins` containing comma-separated plugin IDs.\"\n}\n"},"caller":{"type":"direct"}}],"stop_reason":null,"stop_sequence":null,"usage":{"input_tokens":8,"cache_creation_input_tokens":5164,"cache_read_input_tokens":56907,"cache_creation":{"ephemeral_5m_input_tokens":0,"ephemeral_1h_input_tokens":5164},"output_tokens":1,"service_tier":"standard","inference_geo":"not_available"},"context_management":null},"parent_tool_use_id":null,"session_id":"f9f0b142-a898-420f-acf5-389580b751fa","uuid":"5ff30106-0456-4544-a1fb-8d67188de1c0"}

consists of several integrated components that handle manifest signing, signature validation, and unsigned plugin allowlist enforcement.\\n\\n**Manifest Signing and Reading (pkg/plugins/manager/signature/manifest.go):**\\nThe `Signature` type implements the `SignatureCalculator` interface. The `Calculate` method orchestrates the signature verification process by reading the MANIFEST.txt file from each plugin's filesystem using `ReadPluginManifestFromFS`. The manifest is parsed via `readPluginManifest` which uses OpenPGP's clearsign.Decode to extract both the plaintext manifest JSON and the cryptographic signature. The `validateManifest` function verifies the manifest structure contains required fields and calls `Verify` to validate the PGP signature using public keys retrieved via the `KeyRetriever` interface. The `verifyHash` function validates individual plugin file hashes against the manifest's file records using SHA256.\\n\\n**Signature Validation (pkg/plugins/manager/signature/signature.go):**\\nThe `Validation` type implements the `Validator` interface. The `ValidateSignature` method checks if a plugin's signature is valid by examining the `SignatureStatus` field. For unsigned plugins, it consults the `PluginLoaderAuthorizer` via `CanLoadPlugin`. The validator handles signature inheritance for child plugins and returns appropriate errors for invalid, modified, or unsigned plugins.\\n\\n**Unsigned Plugin Allowlist Enforcement (pkg/plugins/manager/signature/authorizer.go):**\\nThe `UnsignedPluginAuthorizer` implements the `PluginLoaderAuthorizer` interface. The `CanLoadPlugin` method checks if an unsigned plugin is permitted by: (1) checking if DevMode is enabled (allows all), or (2) checking if the plugin ID matches any entry in `cfg.PluginsAllowUnsigned`. This allowlist is configured in pkg/setting/setting_plugins.go where it reads the `allow_loading_unsigned_plugins` setting from the INI configuration file.\\n\\n**Key Retrieval (pkg/services/pluginsintegration/keyretriever/):**\\nThe key retrieval system is dual-layered. The static key retriever (pkg/plugins/manager/signature/statickey/static_retriever.go) provides a hardcoded public key with ID '7e4d0c6a708866e7' used for verifying Grafana-signed plugins. The dynamic key retriever (pkg/services/pluginsintegration/keyretriever/dynamic/dynamic_retriever.go) fetches and caches public keys from the grafana.com API (`/plugins/ci/keys` endpoint), storing them in a KeyStore (pkg/services/pluginsintegration/keystore/keystore.go) that uses the infra kvstore. The service wrapper (pkg/services/pluginsintegration/keyretriever/retriever.go) delegates to either dynamic or static retrieval based on configuration.\\n\\n**Plugin Loading Pipeline Integration:**\\nThe bootstrap stage (pkg/plugins/manager/pipeline/bootstrap/steps.go) calls the `SignatureCalculator.Calculate` method during plugin construction to determine each plugin's signature status before it's added to the registry. The validation stage (pkg/plugins/manager/pipeline/validation/steps.go and pkg/services/pluginsintegration/pipeline/steps.go) applies the `SignatureValidationStep` which invokes the `Validator.ValidateSignature` method, rejecting plugins that fail signature verification unless they're in the unsigned allowlist and DevMode is enabled.\\n\\n**Data Models (pkg/plugins/models.go):**\\nPlugins track four signature statuses: `SignatureStatusInternal` (core plugins), `SignatureStatusValid` (valid signature), `SignatureStatusInvalid` (bad signature), `SignatureStatusModified` (valid signature but content mismatch), and `SignatureStatusUnsigned` (no MANIFEST.txt). Signature types include `SignatureTypeGrafana`, `SignatureTypeCommercial`, `SignatureTypeCommunity`, `SignatureTypePrivate`, and `SignatureTypePrivateGlob` for URL pattern matching.\\n\\n**Configuration (pkg/plugins/config/config.go, pkg/setting/setting_plugins.go):**\\nThe `PluginManagementCfg` holds `PluginsAllowUnsigned` (list of plugin IDs allowed to load without signatures), `DevMode` (allows all plugins), and public key retrieval settings.
